| 1:38:49| I'm going to ask Dr. Lyons, just for public information,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5929)|
| 1:38:53| since we're talking about TIFs and pilots, if you would define the difference between the two.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5933)|
| 1:39:01| Sure.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5941)|
| 1:39:02| What happens is, take with a pilot, it's very simpler to get to grasp, I think,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5942)|
| 1:39:07| because what it means is you just freeze the taxes at the present level.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5947)|
| 1:39:11| And whoever owns the property and develops that property doesn't pay the increase| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5951)|
| 1:39:17| that would go with the reappraisal of the property.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5957)|
| 1:39:19| They keep paying it at the present level.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5959)|
| 1:39:22| And then after a number of years, the taxes return and go to what the appraised value would be.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5962)|
| 1:39:28| With a TIF, it is money that the similar thing happens, the taxes are frozen,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5968)|
| 1:39:37| but those dollars the developer uses to get a loan, what's called a TIF loan,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5977)|
| 1:39:42| where future taxes pay that loan off.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5982)|
| 1:39:44| So a TIF is a little more complicated,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5984)|
| 1:39:46| and that allows there to be what's called tax increment financing so that the increase in taxes that do come in,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5986)|
| 1:39:53| the taxes are paid in a TIF where they're not paid in a pilot.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5993)|
| 1:39:56| In a TIF they're paid, but then they're turned around and go back to pay off a loan to help get that project started.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=5996)|
| 1:40:02| So I guess the major difference is in a pilot the taxes are not paid, they're frozen,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=6002)|
| 1:40:06| in a TIF they're paid, but then they are redirected back to the project.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265120403?start=6006)|
